implementation is centered in the ConnectorsResource class (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/resources/ConnectorsResource.java), which implements JAX-RS resource handlers for managing connectors at the HTTP endpoints. This is the primary connector resource handler supporting all connector operations including creation, deletion, configuration, status retrieval, and task management.\\n\\nThe REST API response schemas are defined in multiple entity classes:\\n\\n1. ConnectorStateInfo (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/entities/ConnectorStateInfo.java) - Contains nested TaskState and ConnectorState classes that represent task and connector status. TaskState includes fields: id (int), state (String - values like RUNNING, PAUSED, FAILED), worker_id, msg (trace), and version. ConnectorState includes state, worker_id, msg, and version fields.\\n\\n2. ErrorMessage (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/entities/ErrorMessage.java) - Standard error response with error_code (int) and message (String) fields.\\n\\n3. TaskInfo (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/entities/TaskInfo.java) - Contains task identifier and configuration map.\\n\\nError response generation is handled by ConnectExceptionMapper (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/errors/ConnectExceptionMapper.java), which maps exceptions to ErrorMessage responses with appropriate HTTP status codes.\\n\\nVersion routing and REST server configuration is managed by:\\n- ConnectRestServer (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/ConnectRestServer.java) - Extends RestServer to register all REST resources\\n- RestServer (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/RestServer.java) - Base REST server implementation that registers resource handlers\\n\\nSchema versioning is evident in KafkaConfigBackingStore.java (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/KafkaConfigBackingStore.java) where:\\n- TARGET_STATE_V0: Contains only \\\"state\\\" field (String)\\n- TARGET_STATE_V1: Adds optional \\\"state.v2\\\" field for new state values\\n\\nThis represents schema evolution from v0 to v1 for target state storage. The v1 schema maintains backward compatibility by making the new state.v2 field optional, allowing clients to work with the new field while older instances continue using the state field.\\n\\nThe request flow: HTTP Request -> ConnectorsResource methods -> Herder interface -> ConnectorStateInfo.TaskState response -> ErrorMessage for errors.\\n\\nNote: The codebase does not show separate v1 and v2 REST API endpoint classes. Instead, a single REST API implementation with schema versioning for internal state representation is maintained. Version handling appears to be schema-based rather than endpoint-based.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":0,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1341,"cache_read_input_tokens":106738,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1341},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"ab06ee49-5cc0-456a-915e-e9ad1d13c363","uuid":"80fe22fa-2ec7-4362-9c85-c3c82ba79b78"}
